Exported Tobacco Leaves Can Get Back Half of the Original Special Tax The tobacco leaves produced in our country's Henan, Hubei, Zhejiang, and other provinces are very large in quantity. The tax rates levied have always been administered by the provinces themselves, and the tax rules are heavy, causing hardship for merchants and the people. Since July 1, when the Ministry of Finance ordered reforms, outsiders have generally not been aware of the underlying reasons. Yesterday, the reporter made a special trip to visit Mr. Ding Zhenbo, a standing committee member of the Tobacco Leaf Industry Guild, and asked him for details. Mr. Ding said that regarding the method of collecting tobacco taxes, in the past, stamp duty and alcohol tax were paid in the place of origin, and the rules differed from province to province. For example, Zhejiang Province levied 2.25 yuan per Customs catty every morning, and an additional public sales fee of 0.8 to 2.2 yuan was levied, averaging 1.56 yuan, for a total levy of about 4 yuan. If transported to other provinces, another half of the public sales fee had to be levied at the destination. Such multiple levies on the same item were not only a heavy burden but also caused sluggish sales and losses for merchants. Since the Ministry of Finance ordered the Tax Administration to implement reforms last month, a special tax has been collected at the place of origin at a rate of 4.15 yuan per 100 market catties, equivalent to 5.02 yuan per 100 Customs catties. Transportation and sales to the seven provinces of Fujian, Henan, Jiangxi, Hubei, Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Anhui are generally not subject to repeated levies. Initially, the industry opposed this because the tax rules were heavier than before, and they felt unable to bear the burden during this time of declining tobacco sales. The reporter repeatedly requested a reduction from the Tax Administration, which repeatedly explained in detail that although the tax rules were slightly increased compared to before, they could be sold in seven provinces without repeated levies. After careful consideration, the actual difference was not great, and sales would be much more convenient. Later, the guild continued to petition that if the tobacco was transported and sold outside the seven provinces and abroad, it should be exempted from tax to facilitate sales and expand foreign trade. After the Tax Administration forwarded the petition to the Ministry of Finance for approval, all domestic tobacco, whether sun-cured or smoked, could receive a full refund of the original special tax or consolidated tax from the Tax Administration upon presentation of customs export documents. If domestic tobacco is transported to areas outside the seven provinces, half of the original special tax can also be refunded from the Tax Administration upon presentation of customs tax receipts. At a time when the rural economy is bankrupt and prices are plummeting, Commissioner Xie is considerate of the plight of farmers and businesses and has petitioned on their behalf, allowing our country's domestic products to be sold abroad tax-free. This is part of the government's plan to revitalize the domestic economy and a new initiative to care for the people. Notice from the Cholera Prevention Office No. 3 Shanghai Temporary Cholera Prevention Office Notice No. 3: The Shanghai Temporary Cholera Prevention Office issued its third announcement on September 9, stating: (1) Since the last announcement, it has been five weeks, and there have been no cholera cases in Shanghai. According to past experience, Shanghai has never had a cholera outbreak starting in September, so this year can be called cholera-free. The same situation occurred in 1918. (2) Health agencies across the country are better prepared for cholera prevention than in previous years. However, on July 24, there was a male patient in Wuchang, and on September 5, there was a female patient in Hankou. Both cases were tested and confirmed to be cholera, and both have now recovered. (3) There are many cases of gastroenteritis, dysentery, and typhoid fever in this city and other cities. The cause is unclean drinking water taken from ponds or shallow wells. If there were clean drinking water facilities, most of these cases could be avoided. (4) There are still more than 20 epidemic hospitals in Shanghai, as in previous years, with medical personnel and equipment for cholera treatment. This year, because there have been no true cholera cases, there is little work to do. Most hospitals will close in mid-September. (5) The work of the two subcommittees of this office has been quite successful. The Epidemiology Research Society has tested and checked cholera bacteria and water quality from the Huangpu River, Suzhou Creek, Yangshupu, Xujiahui, Hongkou Creek, and various shallow wells. Because poor people nearby still use this kind of water for drinking, the inspection results did not find cholera vibrio, but there are non-pathogenic vibrio in the water in various places. Four types have now been identified. This work will continue to be studied this year. The Propaganda Committee has prepared to expand propaganda methods based on the past three years of experience. Once cholera occurs, propaganda will be carried out according to this procedure to achieve the purpose of controlling the epidemic. Weather conditions are also related to the occurrence of cholera. In order to study this issue, meteorological reports on Shanghai, Guangzhou, Hankou, Xiamen, Nanjing, Tianjin, and Qingdao have been obtained from the Hong Kong Observatory, Xujiahui Observatory, Guangzhou Zhongshan University Observatory, and Customs Patrol Service. When the temperature is too high, the absolute humidity also increases. When the absolute humidity is as high as 0.4 inches, the epidemic will spread, so the cholera epidemic is related to absolute humidity. However, an increase in humidity is not a precursor to the spread of the epidemic. (6) Preventive injections were still carried out in August as before. From September to the end of July, a total of 165,769,379,696,543,465 people were vaccinated in Shanghai, 55,698,186,371,242,069 people in the public concession, and 16,367,615,127,787,2 people in the French concession. With this result when there is no cholera epidemic, it can be seen that people at all levels of society have great faith in the measures of the health authorities. If there are other epidemics, they can also proceed accordingly. (7) The weather in summer is dry and hot. There was no rain in July, and it only rained after August 12. Although residents drink a lot of raw water and watermelon, there has been no cholera outbreak. If residents can pay attention to eating clean melon fruits and drinking tap water as boiled water, most cholera and other gastrointestinal diseases can be eradicated. The main task of cholera prevention is to establish tap water in various parts of the country, and the people will welcome this kind of clean drinking water to replace the foul-smelling water. (8) If the health authorities can provide clean drinking water, free injections, hospital treatment, and feces disposal, cholera will not be difficult to eradicate in Shanghai. Taiwan, Java, Kota, Singapore, and other places were once cholera-prone areas, but now there is no cholera. This can be used as a reference. (9) If there are no other incidents, this will be the last announcement of the year, and I am deeply grateful to the relevant authorities and health agencies, testing institutes, observatories, etc. in the concession and Shanghai for their assistance. This year, a Chinese and English booklet will be published on cholera symptoms and prevention methods for the reference of all sectors of society. Educational News Ministry of Education Announced Methods for Re-Examination of Students Selected for Overseas Study in Various Provinces and Cities The Ministry of Education formulated six articles on the methods for re-examination of students selected for overseas study in various provinces and cities, which were announced on the 7th by ministerial order. The articles are as follows: (1) The Ministry of Education shall organize a re-examination committee for the selection of students for overseas study in various provinces and cities in accordance with the provisions of Article 7, Section 2 of the Overseas Study Regulations to handle re-examination matters. (2) The members of the re-examination committee shall be appointed and employed by the Minister of Education at each re-examination session, and the Director of the relevant department shall be the Chairman. (3) The re-examination committee shall be responsible for reviewing the grades of the students selected for the preliminary examination submitted by various provinces and cities and for the re-examination questions and grading matters. The relevant department shall be responsible for reviewing the various documents of the students selected for the preliminary examination. (4) The re-examination results shall be evaluated by the re-examination committee and submitted to the Minister of Education for approval. (5) The date, location, and subjects of the re-examination shall be announced by the re-examination committee in the newspaper. (6) These methods shall be implemented by the Ministry of Education upon announcement. On the Essence of Free Will vs. Determinism, by Qifan

Chinese people are, by and large, determinists. Most believe that one's fortunes, longevity, and destiny are predetermined by one's birth chart (八字). Fortune tellers even use the calculation of these charts to make a living, while also explaining the inevitable reasons why the rich are rich, the poor are poor, and the powerful are powerful. This principle is beyond doubt and can never be wrong. It is the destiny assigned by the Creator at the time of one's birth, decreeing that one will starve to death, even with copper mountains like Deng Tong; that even an emperor like Emperor Wu of Liang cannot avoid it; and that one will soar to great heights, even if one was once a small novice monk selling himself in a temple like Zhu Yuanzhang, who became an emperor.

If a person's circumstances are good, it is because their destiny dictates it. If a person becomes a high-ranking official, it is because their destiny dictates it. If a person is poor, it is due to their bad fate. If a person is beheaded, it is also their destiny. Everything is predetermined by the Creator. The wealth of the rich, the blessings of the fortunate, and the suffering of the miserable are all predetermined, as they should be and must be. Therefore, while wine and meat rot behind red doors, and there are corpses by the roadside, one can only view it as a difference in fate, a contrast between the blessings of the fortunate and the suffering of the miserable, and one cannot seek any connection between them. If one thinks about issues of distribution, wanting to give the uneaten meat and wine to the starving, it is divinely forbidden.

The recent widespread advocacy for rescuing the decline of Chinese rural villages is nothing more than the heavenly mandate for the suffering people in rural areas to suffer even more because they only have the fate of suffering, and they can never improve no matter what. Under such a heaven-ordained organization and distribution method, even if industry were to be revitalized a hundredfold, the suffering would still suffer, and perhaps suffer even more miserably. If one thinks that having enough resources for everyone to eat and use means that everyone can eat when there is enough, then shouldn't it also mean that everyone should eat less when there is not enough? Why did Mencius have to say, "In the kitchen there is fat meat, in the stable there are fat horses, yet on the road there are starved corpses, and the people have famine in their faces?"

The essence is very refined: those who can enjoy blessings can enjoy blessings everywhere, and those who are destined to suffer can only suffer everywhere. Before the theory of determinism is broken down, all forms of relief, revitalization, and reform are futile. Because under this established theory of determinism, these methods can never reverse the situation to make the suffering enjoy blessings and the blessed suffer, but will only continue to make the blessed enjoy more blessings and the suffering suffer more. Here, I realized that the "fate" in "revolution" is the same as the "fate" in "determinism." It seems that the revolution has already succeeded, but seeing the large number of fortune tellers still in business now makes me feel very strange.

"Take Off the Hair on My Face" 152

Lin Yutang

Mr. Qian Gechuan, in a recent "Free Talk," stated that I fabricated evidence in my criticism of Basic English, claiming that the examples from certain pages of the book "Carlo and Anna" (Carland Anna) that I cited were not found in the book (I don't have the original text at hand, but that's the gist). The page numbers I based on were from Ogden's original work, "A Basic Vocabulary," and if there were errors in the page numbers, Ogden should be responsible. It's likely a different edition. Now, I will again refer to the 1930 edition of "Carlo and Anna" (translated by L.W. Lockhart, published by Kegan Paul in London, with a preface by Ogden), specifying the page numbers to prove that my words are not false, and also attach a few strange new discoveries. Mr. Qian says it's not there; I say it is. If it cannot be resolved in the future, we will have to ask Mr. Li Liewen to treat us to a meal to settle this case.

The examples I pointed out in the original text (The Analects, Issue 22), totaling five, are all here.

(1) Regarding the phonograph: "a polished black circle, with a picture of a dog in front of a horn, was playing a piece of military music" (pages 51, lines 8-10).

(2) Regarding beard: Not only is there no word for "beard," there is not even a word for "shave." Therefore, there is a passage saying that when Carlo was in prison, he "taken the hair off his face every Saturday" (page 28, last line). "Hair on the face" is also seen on page 18, line 7 ("the hair on his face was long and untended"); page 58, line 11 ("the shopkeeper once had black hair on his upper lip"); page 29, lines 2-4 ("If you didn't have hair on your face before, and after these years you have hair, go see her...")

(3) Regarding nipple: "Her milk vessels, which were surprisingly young, were white and small and had a mellow sky blue markings" (Forgive my direct translation, because the original text is already awkward; "markings" likely refers to "blue veins") (pages 72, second to fourth lines from the bottom).

In another passage, the original book uses "nipple," but Basic English does not use "milk vessels" but uses "upper part of her body": "The question I frequently put to myself is Why is that the upper part of her body is so white and the rest of her body and her legs a so much deeper colour?" (page 18, lines 12-16).

(4) Regarding fantasy: The most burning thought picture (page 31). Regarding this passage, see below.

(5) Regarding onion: "White root that brings tears to the eyes": This example is Ogden's own explanation of the method of circumlocution (see his book "A Basic Vocabulary," page 83).

In addition, I also discovered five incomprehensible and ridiculous sentences in the book "Carlo and Anna." Assuming these sentences were not in "Basic English" but were found in a student's essay, the teacher would definitely criticize them as incomprehensible without hesitation.

(A) "The weight of his stomach did not go." The original text and surrounding sentences are as follows: Richard had made a picture of the design for him. The weight of his stomach did not go. He had an impulse to go and come back easier (page 30, lines 10-14). At first glance, it's completely incomprehensible. Later, I discovered that a sentence in the previous paragraph said that Carlo had a certain "thought picture which seemed a weight on his stomach" (same page, line 2).

(B) "The weight of her body was pulled down": The preceding text is about Anna going upstairs to buy meat, but she didn't have enough money and was pondering how to buy enough for both of them to eat. Following that is (awkwardly, according to the original text): "Thought was necessary. Feeling gave place to thought. The weight of her body was pulled down. Her head came up clear and free" (Judging from the situation, it seems to say that she bent over slightly, then seemed to have an idea and raised her head again). Thought was necessary. Feeling gave place to thought. The weight of her body was pulled down. Her head came up clear and free (page 55, lines 10-14).

(C) Take lips: "And when lifting his eyes he saw her lips open waiting for him and took them again no word was said" (page 48, lines 16-19). The phrase "take lips" seems to mean "kiss," but why not use "kiss" when it is in the 850 words? It is unknown whether it is not allowed to use "kiss" as a verb with the past tense suffix "ed."

(D) "His pleasure was in his eyes": This sentence is a bit like broken Chinese spoken by foreigners. His pleasure was in his eyes (page 22, line 1).

(E) "Sometimes the memory of her goes completely": This is an example of circumlocution. Because there is no word for "forget" in the 850 words, this method of circumlocution is used. Sometimes the memory of her goes completely (page 19, lines 2-3).

In conclusion, I hate this kind of writing, whether it's in Chinese or Western languages. Please take the following passage as a representative example:

"And it became clear to him that the most burning thought picture is not equal to a breathing moving living human being the changes of whose face through the blood have a connection with the living heart and are them selves a part of living The form of a human being has separate existence its motion goes through space cutting through" (page 30, end of the passage).

Enough, enough, writers of today are almost finished. Not only can the hair on the face be taken, but even the lips can be taken. In Basic English, which uses eighteen verbs to express all actions in the world, the use of the word "take" is truly vast.

Lifebuoy 153

Posthumous Work of Peng Jiahuang

Two people camped out in a village. The one with a gram of luck, not caring about anything, lay in the middle of the road. The one with a ton of wisdom, afraid of being run over by carriages, lay by the side of the road. Late at night, a carriage came. The two horses, seeing the dark figure in the middle of the road, jumped to the side in fright, instead running over the person with a ton of wisdom. A Romanian proverb says:

"One gram of luck is better than a cartload of wisdom."

A certain newspaper recently published an "interesting story," a "pathetic howl": Xu Mingfu of Jiaxing, unemployed for a long time, extremely bored, wandered back and forth along the Huangpu River. At the wharf, he broke a glass cabinet set up by the roadside, took out a lifebuoy, and was arrested and sent to court. The court, believing that he "misunderstood" the meaning of the word, violated the criminal law and sentenced him to ten days of detention, suspended for two years. After the sentence was pronounced, he was dismissed.

In the world, people often find life in death. Like an ostrich that doesn't resist, burying its head in the sand to avoid death, it can't escape death in the end. If a person is still "alive" on the shore and takes a lifebuoy meant for drowning, they are clearly joking with the lifebuoy. Lifebuoys don't care about the lives of people on shore. Only if you want to die in the water will it prevent you from dying.

If Xu Mingfu were truly unafraid of death and jumped into the Huangpu River, perhaps the lifebuoy would be around his neck and he would be saved. If the court had been strict and truly sentenced him to ten days of detention without suspending it for two years, he would at least be saved for those ten days. "After the sentence was pronounced, he was dismissed." The future is vast and uncertain, neither dead nor alive. Where will he go?

People should still rely on a gram of luck and lie in the middle of the road!

Elegy for Peng Jiahuang 154

He Ru

He was worthy of his poor friends,

He was someone who had also gone hungry.

He was worthy of the brave warriors,

He was someone who had also been in prison.

He left behind many readable words,

Yet he never boasted of being a genius.

He participated in many human endeavors,

Yet he was never called a talented person.

He sold much mental labor,

Yet he never sold his own personality.

He was a person who had gone hungry,

He can say goodbye to his poor friends.

He was a person who had been in prison,

He can say goodbye to the brave warriors.

Women (17)

Shen Congwen

The woman said with a smile:

"If you don't love, I will understand without you saying it. Love can also be expressed without words."

The man said:

"Are you still angry with me?"

The woman said:

"What am I angry with you about? What's the point of being angry?"

Later, the two had dinner under the kerosene lamp. After dinner, the woman, as instructed by the doctor, mixed two kinds of medicine into a small bottle, gently shook it for a while, and then poured it into a white porcelain cup.

After taking the medicine, the man lay on the bed, and the woman sat beside the bed, talking to him about everything in the past. When the two talked about the misunderstanding when they separated at the beach in the past, the man said to the woman:

"… Didn't you say you'd give me another chance to prove what kind of person you are? I ask you, what kind of chance is it?"

The woman didn't say anything, stood up for a moment, then sat down again, and pressed her face close to the man's face. The man only felt intoxicated by the fragrance, as if he had never smelled this kind of fragrance before.

The next morning, at about eight o'clock, when the man woke up, the woman was not in the room. There was a small envelope beside the pillow. The outside was not addressed, but he knew that there was a letter inside the white envelope when he touched it. He tore off the paper of the envelope, and sure enough, there was a piece of white paper with writing on it. The letter read:

I don't know why, but I always feel it's better to leave. For my happiness, for not wronging my own feelings, I left. Don't think about any past pain. Since the past has become the past, it's not worth putting your feelings on it to be tormented. You never understood me in the first place. What I hoped for, and have experienced all the pain for this wish for years, was just for you to understand me. Now that you have understood me and loved me, in order to explain our lives more beautifully, it is better for me to leave than for me to live with you.

Your medicine is already prepared on the table. Take it properly according to the doctor's instructions, and then sleep quietly. Learn to be a man, learn to be the kind of man you usually think of yourself as, don't be alarmed, don't let the hotel know anything. I hope you can be as usual, don't worry about me. I didn't leave to increase your longing for me. I just feel that our affair has come to a conclusion, I should leave, so I left.

May God bless you. Ruliu

After reading the letter, he quickly pressed the electric bell by the bed. When the bellboy came, he was still clutching the letter in his hand, lying in bed. He originally wanted to ask the bellboy when the woman who shared the room went down the mountain, but when he saw the bellboy, he didn't say a word, just motioned with his head for him to leave. After the bellboy closed the door and left, he reached out to grab the medicine bottle. The white liquid in the medicine bottle gave off small bubbles when shaken.

He watched these bubbles disappear after being shaken and then stopping, and continued to shake it. He loved her, and felt that he truly loved her. (End)

Customs Seizes Military Arms 155

After a steamship arrives in Shanghai, the Jianghai Customs routinely sends inspectors aboard to check for smuggled prohibited items and contraband military arms. Customs officers, as it is their duty, conduct strict inspections. On the "Green Hogland" steamship, customs officers discovered a large quantity of military arms in the fire hold. It is reported that there were thirty-nine automatic modern firearms and thirty-nine boxes of ammunition for these firearms, totaling four thousand rounds. The military arms were generally loaded in Europe for Shanghai, hoping to be offloaded in Shanghai. Unexpectedly, they were seized by customs.

Investigation into Smugglers 156

When customs inspectors discovered these military arms, they immediately transferred all the firearms and ammunition to a small customs launch, brought them back to customs, and reported to the Tax Commissioner. Simultaneously, they began investigating the individuals involved in the smuggling. On-site investigation revealed a Chinese fireman in the ship's fire hold as highly suspicious. Customs officers brought him to customs for questioning to investigate the origin of the arms. Yesterday, it was also reported that two crew members were summoned by customs for questioning. The specifics of the situation are difficult to fully ascertain. Yesterday, the ship owner reported the matter to the Shanghai shipping authorities. It is said that these military arms were smuggled by crew members and are not directly related to the company or the ship.

Shi Yunchang's Calcium Carbide Experiment Achieves Excellent Results 158

The preparatory work for the China Calcium Carbide Factory has been underway for more than a month. The initiators, Huang Yanfang, Yu Zuoting, Jin Tingsun, Shi Zhikun, Xue Runsheng, Wu Guochang, and others, are all highly respected figures of the time. Calcium carbide (Calcium Carbide) plays an important role in industry. It is an essential raw material for welding steel components, manufacturing acetic acid, rayon, nitrogen fertilizer, aircraft lacquer, and military explosives. Therefore, all countries consider calcium carbide a key national defense item. Recently, electrical and chemical engineer Shi Yunchang has prepared electrical equipment and conducted careful experiments, achieving remarkable results. Yesterday afternoon at 4:00 PM, a public experiment was held on the fourth floor of the Ningbo Native Place Association in Shanghai. Guests from all walks of life arrived in a continuous stream. Mr. Shi arranged the equipment and carried out the production of a small amount of calcium carbide. After about an hour, it was completely successful. He then tested the self-made calcium carbide and imported first-class products using the same amount. The gas produced (i.e., calcium carbide gas) showed that imported products could produce 290 cc of gas per gram of calcium carbide, while domestically produced calcium carbide produced 450 cc of gas, which is superior to imported products. Spectators expressed their admiration. The future success of the factory will greatly benefit China's military and industrial prospects.
